        <div class="dimayor-modal-container" style="display: none;">
            <div class="dimayor-modal-backdrop"></div>
            <div class="dimayor-modal" aria-hidden="true">
                <header>
                    <h3 class="dimayor-modal-title">Detalles del Partido</h3><button class="modal-close"
                        aria-label="Cerrar">✕</button>
                </header>
                <div class="modal-body">
                    <div class="dimayor-tabs">
                        <button class="dimayor-tab is-active" data-tab="eventos">Eventos</button>
                        <button class="dimayor-tab" data-tab="nominas">Alineación</button>
                        <button class="dimayor-tab" data-tab="arbitros">Árbitros</button>
                    </div>
                    <div class="dimayor-tabs__panels">
                        <div class="dimayor-tabpanel is-active" data-remote="eventos"></div>
                        <div class="dimayor-tabpanel" data-remote="nominas"></div>
                        <div class="dimayor-tabpanel" data-remote="arbitros"></div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

    <script>
        (function () {
            const ajax_url = "https://dimayor.com.co/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php";
            const nonce = "40cdb5736d";

            if (!window.updateHoyContent) {
                window.updateHoyContent = async function (wrapper) {
                    if (!wrapper) return;
                    const contentLoader = wrapper.querySelector('.content-loader-container');
                    contentLoader.innerHTML = '<p>Cargando partidos...</p>';

                    const activeDateBtn = wrapper.querySelector('.dimayor-date-btn.active');
                    const dateOffset = activeDateBtn ? activeDateBtn.dataset.dateOffset : '0';

                    const formData = new FormData();
                    formData.append('action', 'get_hoy_matches_ajax');
                    formData.append('nonce', nonce);
                    formData.append('date_offset', dateOffset);
                    formData.append('is_live', wrapper.closest('.dimayor-plugin-wrapper').dataset.isLive || '0');

                    try {
                        const response = await fetch(ajax_url, { method: 'POST', body: formData });
                        const data = await response.json();
                        contentLoader.innerHTML = data.success ? data.data.html : '<p>Error al cargar los partidos.</p>';
                    } catch (error) {
                        console.error("Error al cargar partidos:", error);
                        contentLoader.innerHTML = '<p>Error al cargar los partidos.</p>';
                    }
                };
            }

            // Solo registrar el código base una vez
            if (window.dimayorWidgetInitialized) {
                // Si ya está inicializado, solo ejecutamos la carga inteligente para los nuevos wrappers
                if (typeof runSmartLoad === 'function') {
                    document.querySelectorAll('.dimayor-main-tab-content.active .dimayor-inner-wrapper').forEach(w => {
                        if (w.dataset.competitionTypeName === 'HOY') {
                            window.updateHoyContent(w);
                        } else {
                            runSmartLoad(w);
                        }
                    });
                }
                return;
            }
            window.dimayorWidgetInitialized = true;

            // Delegación de eventos para clics
            document.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                const tabLink = e.target.closest('.dimayor-main-tab-link');
                if (tabLink) {
                    const wrapper = tabLink.closest('.dimayor-plugin-wrapper');
                    const topHoyBtn = wrapper.querySelector('.dimayor-top-hoy-btn');
                    if (topHoyBtn) {
                        topHoyBtn.classList.remove('active');
                    }
                    switchMainTab(tabLink);
                    return;
                }

                const topHoyBtn = e.target.closest('.dimayor-top-hoy-btn');
                if (topHoyBtn) {
                    const wrapper = topHoyBtn.closest('.dimayor-plugin-wrapper');
                    if (topHoyBtn.classList.contains('active')) return;

                    // Desactivar pestañas normales
                    wrapper.querySelectorAll('.dimayor-main-tab-link').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
                    topHoyBtn.classList.add('active');

                    // Ocultar todos los contenidos y activar el de HOY
                    wrapper.querySelectorAll('.dimayor-main-tab-content').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('active'));
                    const hoyContent = wrapper.querySelector('.dimayor-main-tab-content[data-content-type="HOY"]');
                    if (hoyContent) {
                        hoyContent.classList.add('active');
                        const innerWrapper = hoyContent.querySelector('.dimayor-inner-wrapper');
                        if (innerWrapper) {
                            window.updateHoyContent(innerWrapper);
                        }
                    }

                    const color = topHoyBtn.dataset.color || '#023171';
                    document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--dimayor-accent', color);
                    return;
                }

                const dateBtn = e.target.closest('.dimayor-date-btn');
                if (dateBtn) {
                    const wrapper = dateBtn.closest('.dimayor-inner-wrapper');
                    if (dateBtn.classList.contains('active')) return;
                    wrapper.querySelectorAll('.dimayor-date-btn').forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
                    dateBtn.classList.add('active');
                    window.updateHoyContent(wrapper);
                    return;
                }

                const innerTabLink = e.target.closest('.dimayor-inner-tab-link');
                if (innerTabLink) {
                    const wrapper = innerTabLink.closest('.dimayor-inner-wrapper');
                    if (innerTabLink.classList.contains('active')) return;
                    wrapper.querySelectorAll('.dimayor-inner-tab-link').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
                    innerTabLink.classList.add('active');
                    updateContent(wrapper);
                    return;
                }

                const filterToggle = e.target.closest('.filters-toggle-button');
                if (filterToggle) {
                    const nav = filterToggle.closest('.dimayor-inner-nav');
                    if (nav) nav.classList.toggle('filters-open');
                    return;
                }
            });

            // Delegación de eventos para cambios en filtros
            document.addEventListener('change', function (e) {
                const wrapper = e.target.closest('.dimayor-inner-wrapper');
                if (!wrapper) return;

                if (e.target.classList.contains('season-filter')) {
                    updateCompetitions(e.target);
                } else if (e.target.classList.contains('competition-filter')) {
                    updatePhases(e.target);
                } else if (e.target.classList.contains('phase-filter')) {
                    updateMatchdays(e.target);
                    updateContent(wrapper);
                } else if (e.target.classList.contains('matchday-filter')) {
                    updateContent(wrapper);
                }
            });

            window.runSmartLoad = async function (wrapper) {
                if (!wrapper || wrapper.dataset.initialized) return;
                wrapper.dataset.initialized = 'true';

                const seasonFilter = wrapper.querySelector('.season-filter');
                const competitionFilter = wrapper.querySelector('.competition-filter');
                const contentLoader = wrapper.querySelector('.content-loader-container');

                contentLoader.innerHTML = '<p>Detectando competición activa...</p>';

                const formData = new FormData();
                formData.append('action', 'get_active_filters');
                formData.append('nonce', nonce);
                formData.append('season_id', seasonFilter.value);
                formData.append('competition_type', wrapper.dataset.competitionTypeName);

                try {
                    const response = await fetch(ajax_url, { method: 'POST', body: formData });
                    const smartData = await response.json();

                    if (smartData.success) {
                        const { competition_id, phase_id, matchday } = smartData.data;
                        await updateCompetitions(seasonFilter, competition_id);
                        await updatePhases(competitionFilter, phase_id, matchday);
                    } else {
                        updateCompetitions(seasonFilter);
                    }
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error("Error durante la carga inteligente:", error);
                    updateCompetitions(seasonFilter);
                }
            };

            function switchMainTab(tab) {
                if (tab.classList.contains('active')) return;
                const container = tab.closest('.dimayor-plugin-wrapper');
                container.querySelectorAll('.dimayor-main-tab-link, .dimayor-main-tab-content').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active'));
                tab.classList.add('active');

                const color = tab.dataset.color || '#023171';
                document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--dimayor-accent', color);

                const content = container.querySelector(`.dimayor-main-tab-content[data-content-type="${tab.dataset.tabType}"]`);
                if (content) {
                    content.classList.add('active');
                    const wrapper = content.querySelector('.dimayor-inner-wrapper');
                    if (wrapper) {
                        if (tab.dataset.tabType === 'HOY') {
                            window.updateHoyContent(wrapper);
                        } else {
                            runSmartLoad(wrapper);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            async function updateCompetitions(seasonSelect, preselectCompetitionId = null) {
                const wrapper = seasonSelect.closest('.dimayor-inner-wrapper');
                const competitionFilter = wrapper.querySelector('.competition-filter');
                const contentLoader = wrapper.querySelector('.content-loader-container');

                competitionFilter.innerHTML = '<option>Cargando...</option>';
                competitionFilter.disabled = true;
                if (!preselectCompetitionId) contentLoader.innerHTML = '<p>Cargando competiciones...</p>';

                const formData = new FormData();
                formData.append('action', 'get_competitions_for_season_ajax_v5');
                formData.append('nonce', nonce);
                formData.append('season_id', seasonSelect.value);
                formData.append('competition_type', wrapper.dataset.competitionTypeName);

                const response = await fetch(ajax_url, { method: 'POST', body: formData });
                const data = await response.json();

                competitionFilter.innerHTML = '';
                if (data.success && data.data.length > 0) {
                    data.data.forEach(comp => {
                        competitionFilter.innerHTML += `<option value="${comp.id}">${comp.name}</option>`;
                    });
                    competitionFilter.disabled = false;
                    competitionFilter.style.display = data.data.length > 1 ? 'inline-block' : 'none';
                    if (preselectCompetitionId) competitionFilter.value = preselectCompetitionId;
                    if (!preselectCompetitionId) await updatePhases(competitionFilter);
                } else {
                    contentLoader.innerHTML = '<p>No hay torneos para esta temporada.</p>';
                    wrapper.querySelector('.phase-filter').innerHTML = '<option>— Fase —</option>';
                    wrapper.querySelector('.matchday-filter').innerHTML = '<option>— Jornada —</option>';
                }
            }

            async function updatePhases(competitionSelect, preselectPhaseId = null, preselectMatchday = 0) {
                const wrapper = competitionSelect.closest('.dimayor-inner-wrapper');
                const phaseFilter = wrapper.querySelector('.phase-filter');
                phaseFilter.innerHTML = '<option>Cargando...</option>';
                phaseFilter.disabled = true;
 
                const formData = new FormData();
                formData.append('action', 'get_phases_for_competition');
                formData.append('nonce', nonce);
                formData.append('competition_id', competitionSelect.value);

                const response = await fetch(ajax_url, { method: 'POST', body: formData });
                const data = await response.json();

                phaseFilter.innerHTML = '<option value="">— Fase —</option>';
                if (data.success && data.data.length > 0) {
                    data.data.forEach(phase => {
                        phaseFilter.innerHTML += `<option value="${phase.id}" data-matchdays="${phase.matchdays}">${phase.name}</option>`;
                    });
                    phaseFilter.disabled = false;
                    phaseFilter.value = preselectPhaseId ? preselectPhaseId : data.data[0].id;
                    updateMatchdays(phaseFilter, preselectMatchday);
                    updateContent(wrapper);
                }
            }

            function updateMatchdays(phaseSelect, preselectMatchday = 0) {
                const wrapper = phaseSelect.closest('.dimayor-inner-wrapper');
                const matchdayFilter = wrapper.querySelector('.matchday-filter');
                const selectedOption = phaseSelect.options[phaseSelect.selectedIndex];
                const totalMatchdays = parseInt(selectedOption?.dataset.matchdays || 0);

                matchdayFilter.innerHTML = '<option value="0">— Todas —</option>';
                if (totalMatchdays > 0) {
                    for (let i = 1; i <= totalMatchdays; i++) { matchdayFilter.innerHTML += `<option value="${i}">Jornada ${i}</option>`; }
                    matchdayFilter.disabled = false;
                } else {
                    matchdayFilter.disabled = true;
                    matchdayFilter.value = '0';
                }
                if (preselectMatchday > 0 && totalMatchdays > 0) matchdayFilter.value = preselectMatchday;
            }

            async function updateContent(wrapper) {
                const contentLoader = wrapper.querySelector('.content-loader-container');
                const activeTab = wrapper.querySelector('.dimayor-inner-tab-link.active').dataset.type;
                const competitionId = wrapper.querySelector('.competition-filter').value;
                const phaseId = wrapper.querySelector('.phase-filter').value;
                const matchday = wrapper.querySelector('.matchday-filter').value;

                contentLoader.innerHTML = '<p>Cargando...</p>';
                if (!competitionId) { contentLoader.innerHTML = '<p>Por favor, seleccione un torneo.</p>'; return; }

                const formData = new FormData();
                formData.append('action', 'get_dynamic_content_v5');
                formData.append('nonce', nonce);
                formData.append('type', activeTab);
                formData.append('competition_id', competitionId);
                formData.append('competition_type', wrapper.dataset.competitionTypeName);
                formData.append('phase_id', phaseId);
                formData.append('matchday', matchday);
                formData.append('is_live', wrapper.closest('.dimayor-plugin-wrapper').dataset.isLive || '0');

                const response = await fetch(ajax_url, { method: 'POST', body: formData });
                const data = await response.json();
                contentLoader.innerHTML = data.success ? data.data.html : '<p>Error al cargar el contenido.</p>';
            }

            // Polling para actualizaciones en vivo (cada 60 segundos)
            setInterval(function() {
                document.querySelectorAll('.dimayor-main-tab-content.active .dimayor-inner-wrapper').forEach(wrapper => {
                    if (wrapper.dataset.competitionTypeName === 'HOY') {
                        window.updateHoyContent(wrapper);
                    } else {
                        // Refrescar solo si hay una competición y fase seleccionada
                        const competitionFilter = wrapper.querySelector('.competition-filter');
                        const phaseFilter = wrapper.querySelector('.phase-filter');
                        const competitionId = competitionFilter ? competitionFilter.value : null;
                        const phaseId = phaseFilter ? phaseFilter.value : null;
                        if (competitionId && phaseId) {
                            updateContent(wrapper);
                        }
                    }
                });
            }, 60000);

            // Inicialización al cargar el DOM
            document.querySelectorAll('.dimayor-main-tab-content.active .dimayor-inner-wrapper').forEach(w => {
                if (w.dataset.competitionTypeName === 'HOY') {
                    window.updateHoyContent(w);
                } else {
                    runSmartLoad(w);
                }
            });
        })();
    </script>
    </div></div></section><section id="brxe-a77b1b" class="brxe-section bricks-lazy-hidden"><div id="brxe-eb8c8d" class="brxe-container bricks-lazy-hidden"         <script>
            if (typeof bvmTabsInit === 'undefined') {
                var bvmTabsInit = true;
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
                    document.body.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                        if (e.target.classList.contains('bvm-tab-btn')) {
                            var btn = e.target;
                            var targetId = btn.getAttribute('data-target');
                            var bvmContainer = btn.parentElement.parentElement;
                            if (!bvmContainer) return;
                            
                            // Desactivar todos
                            bvmContainer.querySelectorAll('.bvm-tab-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('bvm-active'));
                            bvmContainer.querySelectorAll('.bvm-tab-pane').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('bvm-active'));
                            
                            // Activar el seleccionado
                            btn.classList.add('bvm-active');
                            var pane = bvmContainer.querySelector('#' + targetId);
                            if (pane) pane.classList.add('bvm-active');
                        }
                    });
                });
            }

            .bvm-tab-btn[data-comp='liga_femenina'] { background-color: #d3005a; border-color: #d3005a; }
            .bvm-tab-btn[data-comp='superliga'] { background-color: #0054b8; border-color: #0054b8; }

            .bvm-tab-btn.bvm-active { filter: brightness(0.7); box-shadow: 0 4px 6px rgba(0,0,0,0.2); transform: scale(1.02); }
            
            .bvm-tab-pane { display: none; width: 100%; transition: opacity 0.3s ease; }
            .bvm-tab-pane.bvm-active { display: block; animation: bvmFadeIn 0.5s ease forwards; }
            @keyframes bvmFadeIn { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(5px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }
            @media (max-width: 768px) {
                .bvm-tab-btn { padding: 8px 12px; font-size: 12px; }
            }
        </style>
        <script>
            if (typeof bvmTabsInit === 'undefined') {
                var bvmTabsInit = true;
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
                    document.body.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                        if (e.target.classList.contains('bvm-tab-btn')) {
                            var btn = e.target;
                            var targetId = btn.getAttribute('data-target');
                            var bvmContainer = btn.parentElement.parentElement;
                            if (!bvmContainer) return;
                            
                            // Desactivar todos
                            bvmContainer.querySelectorAll('.bvm-tab-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('bvm-active'));
                            bvmContainer.querySelectorAll('.bvm-tab-pane').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('bvm-active'));
                            
                            // Activar el seleccionado
                            btn.classList.add('bvm-active');
                            var pane = bvmContainer.querySelector('#' + targetId);
                            if (pane) pane.classList.add('bvm-active');
                        }
                    });
                });
            }
        </script>
